        <div id="readme" class="Box-body readme blob js-code-block-container p-5 p-xl-6 gist-border-0">
    <article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><h1 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-sound-voltex-exceed-gear-コナステ-charts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#sound-voltex-exceed-gear-コナステ-charts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Sound Voltex Exceed Gear コナステ Charts</h1>
<p dir="auto"><em>Sound Voltex Exceed Gear コナステ</em>, or SDVX EAC for short, comes with a large catalogue of charts, some of which come with the basic course <em>最初からプレーできます</em>, and some of which come with purchasable packs [<a href="https://p.eagate.573.jp/gate/p/eamusement/coop/list.html?shop=1&amp;category=45&amp;cc=0&amp;ls=2" rel="nofollow">1</a>, <a href="https://p.eagate.573.jp/game/eacsdvx/vi/music/index.html" rel="nofollow">2</a>]. This page contains a table of all charts, as of 2022-01-28, as fetched from the main website [<a href="https://p.eagate.573.jp/game/eacsdvx/vi/music/index.html" rel="nofollow">2</a>]. Ctrl+F can be used to search for a specific chart. This table allows for sorting; just click the header of a column to sort by that column (Made possible by the script from Stuart Langridge)[<a href="https://www.kryogenix.org/code/browser/sorttable/" rel="nofollow">3</a>].  The charts themselves can also be inspected through <a href="https://sdvx.in/" rel="nofollow">sdvx.in</a>.</p>
<h2 dir="auto"><a id="user-content-chart-list" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#chart-list"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.775 3.275a.75.75 0 001.06 1.06l1.25-1.25a2 2 0 112.83 2.83l-2.5 2.5a2 2 0 01-2.83 0 .75.75 0 00-1.06 1.06 3.5 3.5 0 004.95 0l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95-4.95l-1.25 1.25zm-4.69 9.64a2 2 0 010-2.83l2.5-2.5a2 2 0 012.83 0 .75.75 0 001.06-1.06 3.5 3.5 0 00-4.95 0l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 004.95 4.95l1.25-1.25a.75.75 0 00-1.06-1.06l-1.25 1.25a2 2 0 01-2.83 0z"></path></svg></a>Chart List</h2>
